  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

<span id="freeTextContainer13477266059054600329">There is need. And then there is Fate...   <span id="freeText13477266059054600329" style="display:none">There is need. And then there is Fate... Being destined to become some kind of supernatural electrical outlet isn’t exactly awesome—especially when Alexandria’s "other half" is everywhere she goes. Seth’s in her training room, outside her classes, and keeps showing up in her bedroom—so not cool. Their connection does have some benefits, like staving off her nightmares of the tragic showdown with her mother, but it has no effect on what Alex feels for the forbidden, pure-blooded Aiden. Or what he will do—and sacrifice—for her. When daimons infiltrate the Covenants and attack students, the gods send furies—lesser gods determined to eradicate any threat to the Covenants and to the gods, and that includes the Apollyon... and Alex. And if that and hordes of aether-sucking monsters didn’t blow bad enough, a mysterious threat seems willing to do anything to neutralize Seth, even if that means forcing Alex into servitude... or killing her. When the gods are involved, some decisions can never, ever be undone</span>

<div id="review_362189126" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/362189126" />
    <a title="MeMe Belikova First lady Ivashkov" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5484217-meme-belikova-first-lady-ivashkov"><img alt="MeMe Belikova First lady Ivashkov" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1367392298p2/5484217.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/362189126?book_show_action=true">Jul 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MeMe Belikova First lady Ivashkov" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MeMe Belikova First lady Ivashkov" href="/user/show/5484217-meme-belikova-first-lady-ivashkov">MeMe Belikova First lady Ivashkov</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer362189126" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6532566505777004898">First off can I say "Damn Lea, how many times do you have to get your nose broken by Alex to understand, that she is not the one to be messed with!" <br/><br/>YES!!! BAD ASS Alex Andros, is at it again! Kicking more Ass in the sequel to the Covenant series! The story starts off where we left it and that was more training with the Bland but HOTT Aiden and the Snarky and Whitty Apolyon Seth. Alex's ultimate goal in life right now:<b>She must find the power within her and try to stay alive until her eighteenth </b></span>
  <span id="freeText6532566505777004898" style="display:none">First off can I say "Damn Lea, how many times do you have to get your nose broken by Alex to understand, that she is not the one to be messed with!" <br /><br />YES!!! BAD ASS Alex Andros, is at it again! Kicking more Ass in the sequel to the Covenant series! The story starts off where we left it and that was more training with the Bland but HOTT Aiden and the Snarky and Whitty Apolyon Seth. Alex's ultimate goal in life right now:<b>She must find the power within her and try to stay alive until her eighteenth birthday.</b> All of this is going to be hard for Alex, <b>A.</b>Because she just can't stay out of trouble and <b>B.<b>Some people want her DEAD. Continuing onin Alex's kick ass adventure to find out who gets their butt kicked by Alex along the way.<br /><br /><b>Alex Andros:</b> She is MY KIND of character! I love EVERYTHING about her, if I could choose to be any character it would be Rose from VA first and then Alex Andros next(lol). Her character kept me laughing and never bored through the entire book!<br /><br /><b>Lover Boys:</b> Can I say I LOVED Seth more in this book! He is just so caring and funny to where I can't get enough of him! I love the connection between Him and Alex, it was so powerful and I am in love with their chemistry. Aiden.......He is so boring for me, I like him when he is sweet and all but he had no personality at all and I am bored with him at the moment. Come on Aiden spice it up with Alex alil more Please?<br /><br /><b>Master Plan/Story:</b> Was AWESOME!! Armentrout knows how to write some juicy stories! I would definitely say this book was a page turner or screen turner for kindle because I couldn't put it down! Hats off to Jennifer! There alot of twist and turns in this book that are so unexpected and its bound to leave you with your jaw dropped to the floor!<br /><br /><b>Romance:</b> Ohhhh Seth, I love you so much. I have fallen more in love with you and I wish you were mine. That is all :)<br /><br /><b>Action Packed:</b> Too much for me to handle!! There was so much action I couldn't keep up, it was a whirl wind of action! I loved it and need more!<br /><br /><br /><b>What Next?:</b> What I want to see next is Alex, finally let go of Aiden OR some more hot scenes with Seth because I can't get enough of that!<br /><br /><b>Cover Love?:</b> I LOVE these covers! They aren't fancy or flashy but they really fit with this series and I hope they keep them that way.<br /><br />I can't wait for DIETY! I'm so excited to see what is going to happen with everyone after everything has happened! I wanna find out who her dad is and I feel like she might find out in the third book!<br /><br />Rating: Kick ASS<br /><br />Thanks for Listening!<br /><br />-Alice Belikova &lt;3<br /><br /> </b></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="6532566505777004898" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer12398822950531929140">dare i say it!? this may be the one absolute isolated incidence where i dont mind a love triangle?! i dont love it, but i understand it and i dont mind it. so thats an improvement. <br/><br/>i definitely feel a focus change in this sequel, compared to the first book. while there is still action, this feels very character driven and its nice. its nice to get to know the characters more and establish their relationships/bonds with each other. <br/><br/>so while this definitely feels like a filler book in the series, </span>
  <span id="freeText12398822950531929140" style="display:none">dare i say it!? this may be the one absolute isolated incidence where i dont mind a love triangle?! i dont love it, but i understand it and i dont mind it. so thats an improvement. <br /><br />i definitely feel a focus change in this sequel, compared to the first book. while there is still action, this feels very character driven and its nice. its nice to get to know the characters more and establish their relationships/bonds with each other. <br /><br />so while this definitely feels like a filler book in the series, i appreciate the time taken to explore the characters. i dont think i would approve of, or even enjoy, the direction things are going (no matter how predictable it is) had this book not happened. so there that. <br /><br />i also srill wish there was more greek mythology present. i have my fingers crossed for the next book!<br /><br /><b>↠ <i>3.5 stars</i></b></span>

<div id="review_236492914" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/236492914" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/236492914?book_show_action=true">Nov 16, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=general-fantasy-and-mythology">general-fantasy-and-mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=controversial-fanfiction">controversial-fanfiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer236492914" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7142672365950992229"><b>*edit* July 2012*.</b> Sigh. Eff it. I really didn't want to have a star rating on this book because of my mixed feelings (good and bad) but since I'm not risking having yet another review sent to the void, I will award a star rating. <br/><br/><b>Original Review</b><br/><br/>Argh. I am so frustrated right now. No matter how entertaining this book is (and it's a great read), I feel dirty for reading it. Blatant copying should not be rewarded. This is even worse than fan fic to me because no one's getting their efforts credite</span>
  <span id="freeText7142672365950992229" style="display:none"><b>*edit* July 2012*.</b> Sigh. Eff it. I really didn't want to have a star rating on this book because of my mixed feelings (good and bad) but since I'm not risking having yet another review sent to the void, I will award a star rating. <br /><br /><b>Original Review</b><br /><br />Argh. I am so frustrated right now. No matter how entertaining this book is (and it's a great read), I feel dirty for reading it. Blatant copying should not be rewarded. This is even worse than fan fic to me because no one's getting their efforts credited back to them. These are not little coincidences...this is an entire world, race &amp; class system, and several characters. It's kind of a big deal.<br /><br />I'm marking this read for now and will collect my thoughts tomorrow when I'm not so tired.<br /><br />*fast forward*<br /><br />...one day later and I'm still torn. Book 2 didn't have as many similarities to VA, well EXCEPT FOR <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the scene with Caleb which echoed what happened to Mason, also in book 2 of the other series. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Oh wait, and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[the way <s>Rose</s> Alex pursued <s>Dimitri</s> Aiden and he backed off for responsibility's sake. Good lord, talk about Deja Vu. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Even with the story veering off a bit in a new direction, the foundation that was laid in book 1 continues to hold strong in book 2. There's no way to change the characters and racial politics now.<br /><br />Armentrout can write an entertaining story. Every single time I pick up a book of hers, I read until my eyes burn. I have a good time. This author has a writing style which draws you in. It would be a lot easier to drop a series when you're not having such a great time reading it. There are a plethora of series which aren't even 1/10th as entertaining. Anytime I find books that are this easy to latch on to, it makes me want to keep going.<br /><br />Will I continue to read the Covenant series? I honestly don't know. The right thing to probably do would be to decide not to continue.<br /><br />If I do continue, it will be simply as a guilty pleasure and I will find a way to obtain a borrowed copy. Also, if I do decide to continue on, I may possibly choose not to review any future installments, but might just mark them as read for my own records. I don't know if I'll be recommending the books from this point forward.<br /><br />If you are considering reading Covenant but <i>have not</i> read the Vampire Academy series by Richelle Mead, do the right thing and pick up Mead's books first, so you can see who created this world.<br /><br />If you're interested in this author but are unsure if you should read Covenant, try checking out her Lux series instead. There are a few similarities with the Lux world and another book series but the details are so minor and in the background that it didn't really bother me. Armentrout does have talent as a writer and at least I was able to enjoy it more with Lux/Obsidian.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7142672365950992229" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_306118648" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/306118648" />
    <a title="Ezmirelda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3800177-ezmirelda"><img alt="Ezmirelda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1358131158p2/3800177.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/306118648?book_show_action=true">Apr 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ezmirelda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ezmirelda" href="/user/show/3800177-ezmirelda">Ezmirelda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3800177-ezmirelda?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3800177-ezmirelda?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3800177-ezmirelda?shelf=unoriginal">unoriginal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer306118648" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8517660665719316315">**************CAUTION, BELOW CONTAINS SPOILERS************<br/><br/> I went into this book wanting to like it and enjoy it. And I did, I loved it. The tension had me on edge. Seth was amazing and I loved him. Aidan was kind of annoying but I loved him too. I <i> really really</i> wanted to read this book without constantly having the sinking feeling that I’ve already read it before, except written by a different author and with a different name (Vampire Academy). The second book of the Half Blood series was rumo</span>
  <span id="freeText8517660665719316315" style="display:none">**************CAUTION, BELOW CONTAINS SPOILERS************<br /><br /> I went into this book wanting to like it and enjoy it. And I did, I loved it. The tension had me on edge. Seth was amazing and I loved him. Aidan was kind of annoying but I loved him too. I <i> really really</i> wanted to read this book without constantly having the sinking feeling that I’ve already read it before, except written by a different author and with a different name (Vampire Academy). The second book of the Half Blood series was rumored to be more original than the first and because I loved the author’s writing and enjoyed the humor in the first book I wanted to give Book 2 a shot despite my annoyance with book 1. <br /><br /><b>Unfortunately……</b><br /><br />The similarity crisis strikes again!<br /><br />Okay, I’ve given up on trying to separate the two. From now on I will be calling the main character <i>Alexrose</i> because, honestly, they are so alike they might as well be the same person. Also, might as well throw in <i>Aidimitri</i> since Aiden and Dimitri are sometimes even more alike than Alex &amp; Rose are. Just to make this a lot less confusing, cuz I honestly mixed them up throughout the entire book.<br /> <br />Aidimitri breaks Alexrose’s heart by saying they can’t be together anymore because they would get in trouble when the higher ups found out and he lies and tells her he doesn’t love her. *Aww* Now I gave this the benefit of the doubt because a great majority of paranormal YA novels have this type of situation, and honestly I saw this coming from book 1. He leads her on all throughout the book and then he goes cold on her when he realizes he's lost control of his mask. <i>(Again, classic YA paranormal sophomore novel).</i><br /><br /><b>Caleb/ Mason</b> (Alexrose’s best male friend) dies and Alexrose is left emotionally scarred (Book 2 of vampire academy, anyone? This one shocked me senseless. It was the first sign that this book would not go Vampire-Academy-less like I hoped it would). <br /><br />It turns out <b>Lea/ Mia</b> who is a PURE can actually <b>fight</b>. Really…are you kidding me? No no, no, no, no, this is definitely <b>not</b> a coincidence! Mia/Lea, the mean girl Pure, can somehow now fight off Daimons/Strigoi after her parents died? <i>Please</i>.<br /><br />Alexrose then goes to council/court where all the Pures/Moroi’s hate her except for one, which leads me into the next one that threw me over the edge:<br /><br /><b>Introducing the newest stolen character:</b> Laaden AKA Tasha, the only Pure/ Moroi who doesn’t hate all the Halfs/Dhampirs. She also turns out to (might) be evil. Wow! You had me there, I did NOT see that coming. At all. (Very heavy sarcasm there, in case you didn’t notice). <br /><br />Then Alexrose gets an aphrodisiac drink (*cough* necklace) that makes her lusty and she almost ends up going all the way with Seth. (Again, Vampire Academy all over again) <br /><br />Meanwhile, the supernatural bond between Alexrose and <i>Sethalisa</i> (Seth + Lisa) is growing and they’re starting to be able to sense each other’s thoughts and feelings. And whenever Sethalisa is with a person intimately Alexrose can sense it. (Remember the whole Lisa + Chrsitian thing where Alexrose would see every time they were having an intimate moment. Yup Sethalisa for sure guys) <br /><br />Each time these things came up and I kept banging my head against a wall. But, I loved the book and could not stop reading it! <br /><br />I’m starting to think the only reason I like it is because I loved Vampire Academy. I feel kind of torn between wanting to be mad at this book for blatantly copying off of another, and seriously liking it for being so similar to a book I loved. <br /><br />If you miss Vampire Academy, and you don’t mind head-banging similarities, would I recommend this book? Yeah. <br /><br /><b>BUT......</b><br />(now this is a very important <i>but</i>)<br /><br />If you haven’t read all the Vampire Academy books I <s>highly</s> <b>strongly</b> recommend you read those first! <br /><br />Why? Because Half-Blood isn’t nearly half as good as Vampire Academy was. In the VA series I liked the characters a lot better, the setting a lot better, and the plot way better. Everything felt more…<i>alive</i> in the Vampire Academy series. <br /><br /><i>Then</i> after you've read it go on to read Half-Blood as a <s>not-so-very-different</s> not-so-different-at-all spin off series.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8517660665719316315" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer220382178" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7511649604283719037"><b>:There be spoilers here. Be warned!:</b><br/><br/>There is nothing quite like the experience when reading an Armentrout novel. <br/><br/>My Symptoms included; <br/><br/>-Stomach tied in a knot so tight it refuses to loosen till the very last sentence. <br/>-Continuously released a breath I didn't realize I was holding. <br/>-Felt the need to want to rip someones heart out and/or bang my head against a wall (depending on the scene).<br/>-Cried frustrated tears of pure agony or annoyance. <br/>-<i>Glared</i> at the words on the page so <i>hard</i> that I could alm</span>
  <span id="freeText7511649604283719037" style="display:none"><b>:There be spoilers here. Be warned!:</b><br /><br />There is nothing quite like the experience when reading an Armentrout novel. <br /><br />My Symptoms included; <br /><br />-Stomach tied in a knot so tight it refuses to loosen till the very last sentence. <br />-Continuously released a breath I didn't realize I was holding. <br />-Felt the need to want to rip someones heart out and/or bang my head against a wall (depending on the scene).<br />-Cried frustrated tears of pure agony or annoyance. <br />-<i>Glared</i> at the words on the page so <i>hard</i> that I could almost taste sheer-will transforming the words right before my eyes (which.does.not.work).<br />-Whimpered at the thought of actually falling for the guy I <i>planed</i> on hating from minute one. <br />-It left me <i>begging</i> for more!! <br /><br /><b>Pure</b> would be the third novel I've read from Jennifer L. Armentrout and I gotta ask, where have you been all my life??<br />Her books are so dame addictive/ devourable/unputdownable. I swear I could read her stories every single day and it'll still leave me craving for more! What I adore about Jennifer's writing is that she really makes the reader understand the choices these characters are put through. For example; I hate all this tension and meanest that Aiden is giving off, but that whole Hector/Kelia scene really put things in a different perspective and it's like something clicked into place. I don't like it. But I finally get it. Smart cookie. I also love the fact that this women can write one hell of an argument scene. It's heated and passionate and extremely well done.<br />But really, there are so many many reason why I adore this book (series). It's action-punched, it has wickedly fun humor, has this crazy unreachable red-hot romance just brimming to the surface to the point of madness and it reads like a freaken dream. <br /><br />The second installment in the <i>Covenant</i> series was intense and crazy. True, we didn't get a lot of answers to our huge list of questions. The story doesn't quite move forward at this point but the plot has thickened up immensely. Which I find totally necessary. It's frustrating, yes, but it's still necessary to develop these characters in a certain light for us to understand more about them as the series goes on, which I can respect but it still leaves me aching for more.<br /><br />These characters are a freaken blast! Alex is made of pure awesome, but the girl gets in trouble. A lot. You just gotta love this girls spirit and spunk, it's the very best thing about her and I think we're only seeing the beginning of greatness.<br />Aiden in this book, well, pissed me the hell off actually. I love him. Seriously, Aiden all the way, and I know what he did for Alex was the best thing for her (that felt like dirt coming out of my mouth) but that doesn't mean I'm not gonna pout about it.<br />Seth? He's still just as arrogant, rude, obnoxious, pushy and incredibly <i>in.the.way.</i>. I have never in my life <i>wanted</i> to hate a character so badly, but at last, Jennifer is evil and gave the bastard some of the greatest sincere moments, that it actually made me melt. I can't hate him now. But I still want to.<br /><br />The story line is a complete rush. I was in constant doubt, who's the good guy/bad guy here. My emotions were also all over the place. I laughed, I cried <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Caleb, Noooooooooo <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and I swooned like a littlegirl. It's an amazingly put together story with outstanding characters who you can't help give your heart to. <br /><br />I could go on forever glowing about this book, so all I have left to say is that I absolutely loved it. It pissed me off, made me smile and made me shiver and all I want is <b>moremoremore</b>!!<br /><br /><i>
  <b>GAHHHHHHHH!!!! DEITY I NEED YOU!!!!</b>
</i><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer350984715058284880">'There were two types of people in this world, those who sat around a fire, staring into the flames, and those who started the fire. <br/><br/>Seth and I started the fire, and then we danced around it.' <br/><br/>This has got to be one of the best sequels to a book I've ever read. Was it better than the first book? Most definitely! <br/><br/>The characters and their roles have developed so much since the first book it's astonishing. <br/><br/>Alex is seriously like a sassy warrior princess in my opinion. <br/>Aiden is really probably meant</span>
  <span id="freeText350984715058284880" style="display:none">'There were two types of people in this world, those who sat around a fire, staring into the flames, and those who started the fire. <br /><br />Seth and I started the fire, and then we danced around it.' <br /><br />This has got to be one of the best sequels to a book I've ever read. Was it better than the first book? Most definitely! <br /><br />The characters and their roles have developed so much since the first book it's astonishing. <br /><br />Alex is seriously like a sassy warrior princess in my opinion. <br />Aiden is really probably meant to be her soul mate, they are literally perfect for each other and are amazing in combat. <br />Seth is like a really mischievous, and reckless friend to Alex, although I have a feeling sooner or later he is gonna turn into a power hungry Apollyon.. so that's probably gonna pose some problems. <br />I like Seth a bit more in this book than I did in the first but I don't think that Alex and him should be fated to each other, like everyone assumes they should be, they'd be at each other throats half the time. <br /><br />I was heartbroken with what happened to Caleb but what's done is done, unfortunately. Lastly, Alex is going to be one powerful Apollyon when she awakens on her 18th birthday, probably more so than Seth, which would be awesome! <br /><br />The entire story was completely enthralling and it was near impossible to put the book down. Can't wait to continue this series. <br /></span>

<div id="review_187321299" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/187321299" />
    <a title="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life"><img alt="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563622982p2/3024878.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/187321299?book_show_action=true">Jul 22, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Donna {Book Passion For Life}" href="/user/show/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life">Donna {Book Passion For Life}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life?shelf=ya-paranormal-romance">ya-paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life?shelf=for-review">for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024878-donna-book-passion-for-life?shelf=books-i-m-quoted-in">books-i-m-quoted-in</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer187321299" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9197899644715795085"><b>“Ever since I’ve met you, I’ve wanted to break every rule.” Aiden turned away, the muscles in his neck tensing. He sighed. “You’ll become the center of someone’s world one day. And he’ll be the luckiest son of a b*tch on this earth.” – Aiden </b><br/><br/>My initial thoughts after reading <i>Pure</i> were wow, Jennifer L. Armentrout is a genius and now, several months later I was definitely right, because it is the best sequel I have <b>EVER</b> read! <br/><br/>This time around we see Alex training with both Aiden and Seth. Aiden is</span>
  <span id="freeText9197899644715795085" style="display:none"><b>“Ever since I’ve met you, I’ve wanted to break every rule.” Aiden turned away, the muscles in his neck tensing. He sighed. “You’ll become the center of someone’s world one day. And he’ll be the luckiest son of a b*tch on this earth.” – Aiden </b><br /><br />My initial thoughts after reading <i>Pure</i> were wow, Jennifer L. Armentrout is a genius and now, several months later I was definitely right, because it is the best sequel I have <b>EVER</b> read! <br /><br />This time around we see Alex training with both Aiden and Seth. Aiden is still trying to get her caught up on the work she missed and Seth is training her to become the future Apollyon. No one said it was going to be easy - and for Alex is isn’t, especially when she becomes targeted by someone who is trying to get her kicked out of the Covenant. Alex can’t help but question who’s behind it? but with danger around every corner for Alex she soon has something else to worry about and that is, can she stay safe from the biggest danger of all; the Furies - who have arrived after daimons attack the students at the Covenant? <br /><br /><i>Pure</i> is undoubtedly one of my favourite reads so far this year and it really surpassed my expectations. Jennifer’s work continues to amaze me and if anything her work gets better and better with each book I read. She manages to create the perfect blend of paranormal, romance and excitement, mixed with pure perfection and I absolutely adored every single minute. <br /><br />The characters as ever do not let us down. Alex is as feisty and strong as always and she really goes through an even tougher time in this book. There’s so many things happening in her life that she cannot control and for some reason she is in the middle of everything. But with Alex being Alex, through out all these hard times she stays true to herself even if it does land her in even more trouble. She’s her fun, witty self and I really admire her - she’s a fantastic heroine!<br /><br />Seth is amazing! I loved him from the first moment I met him and if anything I love him that much more this time around. His and Alex’s relationship takes so many twists during this book and it was really nice to see a different side of him. He’s still as comical as ever and I felt it was a great addition. <br /><br />Now Aiden….I cannot even put into words how much I am in love with this guy, seriously he’s so swoon-worthy that I almost had to wipe the drool off of my mouth. His love for Alex really shows in this book and even though he does do things that make you really angry with him, you really can’t stay made at him for long because he’s doing what he thinks is best….even if that means pushing away the one person he loves more than anything. He’s such an admiral character and you really see the levels he will go to protect Alex and it makes me love him even more. So even though Seth did make his way into my heart, I will always be Team Aiden! <br /><br />The story itself was as dangerous as ever, with twists and turns through-out that really leave you speechless. It’s fast paced, exciting and so, so intense and there’s so much heat between these characters that you can almost feel the book burning in your hand. Honestly, Jennifer doesn’t disappoint one bit and she has completely raised the bar for Deity. I cannot wait to get my hands on it. <br /><br />Now, I need answers.... I’m left with so many questions........who is really after Alex? Will Alex and Aiden ever be together? Will the Covenant ever be safe? But most importantly will the rule on Pure’s and Half-Blood’s being together ever be thrown out? So, so many questions and I’m counting down the days until I finally get my answers. <br /><br />Overall, The Covenant series is definitely one of my favourite series with <i>Pure</i> being my favourite sequel and I highly recommend this series to anyone. <br /><br /><i>A huge, huge thank you to Spencer Hill press for sending me an ARC copy of this book. You guys rock!</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="9197899644715795085" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_616753781" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/616753781" />
    <a title="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies"><img alt="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1500999223p2/4527753.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/616753781?book_show_action=true">May 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" href="/user/show/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies">Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=boarding-school">boarding-school</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=b-word-heroine">b-word-heroine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer616753781" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9398593409957994103">Purely out of curiosity, I'm continuing on with what I feel like is a faint shadow of the Vampire Academy series. In this book, Alex continues on with her training, snarks off even more to Seth/her instructors/everyone in a position of power, despite knowing what's in store for her if she gets in further trouble (mindless servitude to Pures). The plot is also gaping with holes; several important plot points never got resolved in my mind. They were just presented, then seemingly forgotten about t</span>
  <span id="freeText9398593409957994103" style="display:none">Purely out of curiosity, I'm continuing on with what I feel like is a faint shadow of the Vampire Academy series. In this book, Alex continues on with her training, snarks off even more to Seth/her instructors/everyone in a position of power, despite knowing what's in store for her if she gets in further trouble (mindless servitude to Pures). The plot is also gaping with holes; several important plot points never got resolved in my mind. They were just presented, then seemingly forgotten about through the very end, even if they were a recurring point in the story (the mysterious servants at the New York Covenant, for one).<br /><br />I think my main qualm with this book is not so much that it's a copy of another series. I have no problems with that. Masterpieces are influential; great works of arts often start an entire new movement. I don't see the negativity in imitation as long as the imitation is an amazing one. My main problem with this series is the main character, Alex.<br /><br />Alex is such a bloody hypocrite. She loses her temper easily, she is bitchy (admittedly so to herself). She slut shames (calling a rival a skank? Not cool). She repeatedly makes terrible decisions, suffer bad consequences, and then regrets it in hindsight. And still, STILL, after everything she's done, she repeatedly makes the same mistakes, showing no signs that she has learned from her experiences or has matured in any way.<br /><br /><b>"I didn’t think; I just launched my shiny red apple right at her face."</b><br /><br />Yep. She didn't think. It seems to be the recurrent theme in the book.<br /><br />Alex's personality, actions, and beliefs are all contradictory. She is supposed to be an amazing fighter, killing three daimons on her own, yet she can barely hold her own in class.<br /><br /><b>Romvi was an embarrassment to the male race, but he didn’t hear me bitching.</b><br /><br />Calling your instructor names after he beat your ill-prepared ass to the mat. <i>Real</i> mature, Alex.<br /><br />She hates her uncle and stepfather, and refuses to acknowledge the fact that she really owes much to them. Her peers and instructors accuse her of using her influential guardians and family to get out of trouble, and they're right. With all the stupid shit Alex pulls, having the Headmaster as an uncle and the Minister as a stepfather has gotten her out of trouble countless times.<br /><br />When the school seems to be infiltrated by daimons, Alex rebels against the restrictions placed on her and the other half-bloods, even while knowing that the Pures themselves are placed under similar rules. She chafes against the rules and seeks to break then as much as possible. <br /><br />While visiting the zoo, Alex sees the caged animals and observes <b>"Here the animals are safe. Out in the wild, they’d be killing one another or being poached. I know they’ve lost their freedom, but sometimes things have to be sacrificed."</b><br /><br />Uhh...a little contradictory there, Alex? It seems like that's what they're doing at school. Aren't you being a bit of a hypocrite?<br /><br />The list goes on and on. Repeated mistakes, no learning, no maturation.<br /><br /><b>"I should’ve stayed in my room like I was supposed to. There was a reason why a curfew had been imposed. The sanctuary of the Covenant had been violated once. I’d forgotten that, or I just hadn’t thought about it, or cared.<br /><br />I never stopped to think."</b><br /><br />No shit, Sherlock.<br /><br />Despite everything she fails at doing, despite barely being able to hold her own in class, Alex is still queen of the Mary Sues. Without being even a Sentinel, she single-handedly kills daimons, furies...everything they can throw at her. Yeah, I know she's the Apollyon. There has to be some sort of realism in her development as a fighter. To flunk so badly in practice and in class and then become a superhero in the middle of a real fight? Doesn't work that way. I don't buy it.<br /><br />Another thing that irked me...I don't know if it's my version of the e-book that's got the spelling wrong, but the singular for furies is A FURY, not <i>furie</i>.<br /><br />I think I'm done with this series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9398593409957994103" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1054161410" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1054161410" />
    <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict"><img alt="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551124421p2/10717098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1054161410?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780983157236" href="/book/show/13558539-pure">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=paranormal-fantasy">paranormal-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1054161410" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15774729217354973170"><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/ja_zps16dd050b.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410368345i/11098482.jpg' alt=' photo ja_zps16dd050b.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Pure is book two in the Covenant series by Jennifer Armentrout. I love writing my review right after I finish reading a book when my emotions are all still swirling. And right now, let me tell you, my emotions are all over the place.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/pure_zps2da180db.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410912628i/11169091.jpg' alt=' photo pure_zps2da180db.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <br/><br/>Alex has been allowed to stay at the Covenant and start the new semester and continue her training. Not only is she attending classes, she is doing extra training with both Aiden and Seth. She is exhausted. But she wouldn’t give up her time with Aiden for an</span>
  <span id="freeText15774729217354973170" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/ja_zps16dd050b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410368345i/11098482.jpg" alt=" photo ja_zps16dd050b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Pure is book two in the Covenant series by Jennifer Armentrout. I love writing my review right after I finish reading a book when my emotions are all still swirling. And right now, let me tell you, my emotions are all over the place.<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/pure_zps2da180db.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410912628i/11169091.jpg" alt=" photo pure_zps2da180db.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Alex has been allowed to stay at the Covenant and start the new semester and continue her training. Not only is she attending classes, she is doing extra training with both Aiden and Seth. She is exhausted. But she wouldn’t give up her time with Aiden for anything. This is the only real time she has with him. Aiden knows that Alex needs a change of scenery so he takes her for a “mental health day.” It was during this time with him that Alex realized the depth of her feelings.<br><br><b>
  <i>“What expanded in my chest swelled my heart until I felt sure it would burst from my chest, wasn’t a silly crush. It wasn’t just a physical attraction. It was love. I loved Aiden--I loved a pure-blood.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/lab_zpsaa62ce35.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410912628i/11169092.jpg" alt=" photo lab_zpsaa62ce35.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Aiden, though, makes it clear he does not return the feelings and that there will never be anything between them. I do want to say that at times Aiden infuriated me the way he seemed to keep Alex hanging. One look from him and her heart would begin to hope again. Whether or not he has feelings for her, he needs to let her go but in some way he always seemed to rekindle her hope. <br><br><b>
  <i>“He left me spinning in confusion. Hot then cold, kind and then standoffish. I didn’t get it.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/statue_zps5cf19f9e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410912628i/11169093.jpg" alt=" photo statue_zps5cf19f9e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The connection is getting stronger and stronger between she and Seth. And things are seeming to happen ahead of schedule, like her awakening that is supposed to occur on her 18th birthday is somehow beginning now. Seth can sense her emotions no matter where he is and he seems to pop up all of the time. One advantage, though, is that when he is near, she feels calmer. And the only time she can sleep without nightmares is when Seth is with her. And Seth sticks by her through it all. He ends up being her only friend, really. Alex suffers another loss in this book, an agonizing loss. And Seth stays by her side to help her through it. Their relationship is sort of a love/hate relationship. They argue continually but that’s just what they do.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m secure in my awesomeness.” <br><br>“More like you’re secure in your douchiness.”</i>
</b><br><br>Alex still has to attend the big council meeting in New York. She is scheduled to speak about what she learned in Gatlinburg when she was captured by her mother. But there are other forces at play here. There are some including the head minister, Minister Telly, that believe the old ways are the only ways. That the breed order should not be changed. That the Pures are superior and the halfs are nothing. And that the Apollyons are dangerous. Several attempts are made on Alex during her time here. And when she does speak, and tries to warn them of the impending threat from the daimons and the halfs that have been turned, they don’t seem concerned at all. They seem more concerned with trying to prove her a threat. And again, Seth sticks by her throughout.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Was any of this about the heart…or even the body? Or was it just what existed in both of us? The connection, the bond--whatever it was--controlling what we wanted.”</i>
</b><br><br>And then, during a carefree night with Seth:<br><br><b>
  <i>“What are you suggesting?”<br><br>“You choose to see what happens. Between us--you choose us.”</i>
</b><br><br>On top of everything else, the Furies have appeared in the covenants. They are statues of three lesser gods that will break free to protect the pures from daimons or apollyons, whatever the threat may be. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/furies_zpsce220b77.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410912628i/11169094.jpg" alt=" photo furies_zpsce220b77.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Can Alex finally let go of the hope she holds for Aiden and give Seth a chance? Is what is between she and Seth more than just a connection of what they are? Can she even stay alive long enough to find out?<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/torch_zps301821bf.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410912628i/11169095.jpg" alt=" photo torch_zps301821bf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>My review might not seem like it but this particular book is really more action than romance. I really wanted a little more of the mushy stuff. But I still loved every page of it. I did feel quite a lot of frustration with Aiden and have softened a lot towards Seth. And Alex, oh Alex. She is so brave. She makes a lot of decisions in this book that didn’t turn out very well. And I still don’t know who to trust. Her Uncle Marcus or her stepfather, Lucian? I just don’t know. But Alex didn’t ask for any of this. My heart breaks for her. And the way the halfs are treated infuriates me. They are looked upon as nothing. The daimons have figured out a way to infiltrate the Covenants and the halfs want equality. Will Alex even be able to survive until her 18th birthday when she awakens? <br><br><b>
  <i>“You had no other choice.”<br><br>“There are always choices, Seth. There are always choices. I just have this terrible habit of making the wrong ones and now I have to deal with it.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_mocqncejGj1r9ccwso1_500_zpsc5213ec6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410570285i/11125365.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_mocqncejGj1r9ccwso1_500_zpsc5213ec6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15774729217354973170" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1803727174" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1803727174" />
    <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu"><img alt="Ramona Popescu " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594649997p2/33526516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1803727174?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ramona Popescu " href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu">Ramona Popescu </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=hot-romance">hot-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=love-and-action">love-and-action</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=love-this-series">love-this-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=funny-as-hell">funny-as-hell</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=fantasy-paranormal">fantasy-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=man-crush">man-crush</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1803727174" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6416374336609144910">What an amazing series the Covenant isJ I am really excited about every book which I read and it became sort of an addiction, because I literally can’t stop reading it. Jennifer is amazing and this ability of hers to mix romance with action and a dynamic plot is killing me!!<br/><br/>“Pure” is the second book from the Covenant series and although it was not as good as the first one, it had its moments of greatness that were fantastic and breath-taking, not to mention that I love Alex and Aiden as a couple</span>
  <span id="freeText6416374336609144910" style="display:none">What an amazing series the Covenant isJ I am really excited about every book which I read and it became sort of an addiction, because I literally can’t stop reading it. Jennifer is amazing and this ability of hers to mix romance with action and a dynamic plot is killing me!!<br><br>“Pure” is the second book from the Covenant series and although it was not as good as the first one, it had its moments of greatness that were fantastic and breath-taking, not to mention that I love Alex and Aiden as a couple :) <br><br>Alex is dealing with her “second Apollyon” status and this implies having Seth all around her kind like 24/7. Not to mention that his flirty ways are beginning to have an effect on her and because of this, Alex is very uncertain about her feelings. One moment she wants to punch him and the next she is very attracted to him. The bond that they share is scary and uncontrollable and she is months from Awakening, things that scares her off her mind. In her personal life things are not getting better, Aiden is still fighting his feelings for her and this is killing her because she knows something is there, she can feel it, but the rule that Pures and Halfs are not allowed to love each other is keeping them apart. Tragic things will happen, that will change Alex irrevocably and many will see her as a threat, something that has to be terminated before it is too late.<br><br>The plot was not sooo dynamic as the first book, there were certain moments when I felt very enraptured in the plot and couldn’t breathe, but those were kind of scattered ( I can name max. 3 great moments). This book was more for exploring and figuring things out, not very alert, but deep. <br><br>Alex is a whirlwind, a twister in feelings and actions, she made me laugh, made me so mad at her, but at the end of the day, she had the right to make mistakes, because as you know, nobody is perfect. In “Pure” she will face a lot and will lose people she loves, but this ability to go forward, to rise, was amazing. She is very strong and I enjoyed seeing her in her tops and lows moments. There is definitely an evolution there, it is palpable and anyone can see it. She is afraid of what she will become, but in her way, she’s finding the way to cope with it. Her forbidden love for Aiden and her attraction and uncertainties towards Seth make her human, but also confuses the Hell out of you. She is really unpredictable, like a storm changing its course constantly, but I like her, I liked that spark and consider her not a typical heroine. <br><br>Even if I read “Titans” first, I wasn’t feeling the connection with Seth and I believed that once reading “Covenant” my opinion will change, but guess what? It didn’t :) I am Team Aiden all the way, even if Seth is greater, more powerful yada yada. I don’t trust him, not feeling anything he says and I just want him far from Alex.<br><br>Now Aiden here is another story, I liked him like instantly, but in this book I really feel like punching him. Why follow the rules Aiden when you love Alex??? I wanted him to take some courage from Alex and just finish already what we know is unavoidable. In “Pure” he is more distant from Alex, more keen on doing the right thing, even if this means confusing her with mix signals and making he choose Seth attention as plan B. By the end of the book Aiden will do something that shocks all of us, but made me love him more, seeing that his wall can be cracked, because at the end of the day, love is always first. I have a feeling that in the third book, his attitude will be totally different towards Alex and finally we will see him take some action and man up, even if he knows it is against the rules.<br><br>So, a good book, it could have been better, but I love the series and I will consider it as a whole. Take this as a transition book, that will lead to amazing things in Deity, the third one. A very addictive series, which I highly recommend it to all of you:)<br><br>4 stars!<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479123324i/21149668._SX540_.png" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews please check <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com">https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6416374336609144910" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11098567235500911910">4 Stars!<br/><br/><b>*I'M GONNA MAKE A FULL REVIEW WHEN I FINISH THIS SERIES*</b> <br/><br/><br/>I actually liked this one better than the first one! There was more action, and well, in this book we have more of Seth, yay! However I'm not giving this book 5 stars for several reasons: <br/><br/>- First, the love triangle. I strongly dislike love triangles, when a heroine finds herself in that situation, her inner-monologue becomes annoying and my eyes start hurting from rolling them so much. <br/><br/>- Second, Aiden. I don't know... I can't conne</span>
  <span id="freeText11098567235500911910" style="display:none">4 Stars!<br /><br /><b>*I'M GONNA MAKE A FULL REVIEW WHEN I FINISH THIS SERIES*</b> <br /><br /><br />I actually liked this one better than the first one! There was more action, and well, in this book we have more of Seth, yay! However I'm not giving this book 5 stars for several reasons: <br /><br />- First, the love triangle. I strongly dislike love triangles, when a heroine finds herself in that situation, her inner-monologue becomes annoying and my eyes start hurting from rolling them so much. <br /><br />- Second, Aiden. I don't know... I can't connect with him? Believe me, I tried, but everytime I read his moments with Alex I feel like falling asleep. Although, I must say that in the end of the book I started liking him a little bit more, but still... Meh. <b>TEAM SETH!</b><br /><br />-Third, can Alex stop blaming herself for everything? I hate when something bad happens and there are like 50 chapters of herself crying over someone's death or idk, ugh. I'm sounding like a heartless bitch but I'm sorry, it's so annoying! <br /><br />-Fourth, sometimes the story is too predictable. <br /><br />Anyway, I still love the amazing world JLA created! I am completely absorbed in the story. Can't wait to keep reading this wonderful series!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11098567235500911910" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer87960691594825288"><b>5/5</b><br/><br/>This book was very good. It was a little similar to the Vampire Academy but I was surprised by everything that happened which is very good. I didn't like Aiden as much but then again he is just acting a certain way for the plot. There was an even larger amount of action in this book than in the first, especially at the end. It was so suspenseful and I was trying to read even faster with out skipping over anything important. There is a kind of cliffhanger just because a lot of things were left</span>
  <span id="freeText87960691594825288" style="display:none"><b>5/5</b><br /><br />This book was very good. It was a little similar to the Vampire Academy but I was surprised by everything that happened which is very good. I didn't like Aiden as much but then again he is just acting a certain way for the plot. There was an even larger amount of action in this book than in the first, especially at the end. It was so suspenseful and I was trying to read even faster with out skipping over anything important. There is a kind of cliffhanger just because a lot of things were left unsaid and mysteries that need to be solved. The romance has gotten even better with a love triangle which is not always good but it is when Jennifer Armentrout writes it. Alex is a pretty good character in this but I feel like at times she was acting a little weaker. Overall this was a great book and I can't wait to read the next one. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11360771746921552213"><b>*3.25 SUPERHUMAN STARS*</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“I guess there were two types of people in the world, those who sat around a fire, staring into the flames, and those who started the fire. Seth and I started the fire, and then we danced around it.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Despite the fact that this still reminded me an awful lot of the <i>Vampire Academy</i> series, I still quite enjoyed this! Unfortunately, I've read a lot of Jennifer L. Armentrout books and thus had very high expectations of this series. I hate to say it, but so far I'm a little </span>
  <span id="freeText11360771746921552213" style="display:none"><b>*3.25 SUPERHUMAN STARS*</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I guess there were two types of people in the world, those who sat around a fire, staring into the flames, and those who started the fire. Seth and I started the fire, and then we danced around it.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Despite the fact that this still reminded me an awful lot of the <i>Vampire Academy</i> series, I still quite enjoyed this! Unfortunately, I've read a lot of Jennifer L. Armentrout books and thus had very high expectations of this series. I hate to say it, but so far I'm a little disappointed...<br /><br />Did I mention I hate love triangles? Don't get me wrong, I know Jennifer Armentrout uses that particular trope a lot in her books and I usually enjoy them, but in this case I was just incredibly annoyed! I mean, come on Alex, just <b>MAKE UP YOUR FREAKING MIND ALREADY!</b></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41915343-daniella-reading-with-daniella?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41915343-daniella-reading-with-daniella?shelf=ya-fantasy-dystopian-sci-fi">ya-fantasy-dystopian-sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41915343-daniella-reading-with-daniella?shelf=read-more-than-once">read-more-than-once</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41915343-daniella-reading-with-daniella?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41915343-daniella-reading-with-daniella?shelf=want-to-buy">want-to-buy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41915343-daniella-reading-with-daniella?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1738797932" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3230077444738061315"><a href='https://readingwithdaniella.wordpress.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Click here to see this review and others on my blog Reading With Daniella</a><br/><br/><b> August 2016: </b> Wow, this was fantastic! I think I liked it even better than the last. I flew right through this book, and just could not put it down. Jennifer's writing is just so addictive, not that I'm complaining!<br/><br/>While I am still team Aiden, I have also seriously fallen for Seth. I was sad that there wasn't as much Aiden action in this installment, but I found myself really enjoying the scenes with Alex and Seth. Their c</span>
  <span id="freeText3230077444738061315" style="display:none"><a href="https://readingwithdaniella.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Click here to see this review and others on my blog Reading With Daniella</a><br /><br /><b> August 2016: </b> Wow, this was fantastic! I think I liked it even better than the last. I flew right through this book, and just could not put it down. Jennifer's writing is just so addictive, not that I'm complaining!<br /><br />While I am still team Aiden, I have also seriously fallen for Seth. I was sad that there wasn't as much Aiden action in this installment, but I found myself really enjoying the scenes with Alex and Seth. Their constant bickering and the sarcasm they had with each other was absolutely hilarious. There were also some rather cute and romantic scenes that I couldn't help but swoon over. There was a part where they were dancing together in the courtyard and it was so swoony, until Seth dropped Alex, but I found that to make the scene even more adorable. There was also the scene in the pool after the ball, and it was just perfect. I also loved the part when Alex accidentally had the brew and was acting all loopy. <br />And as much as I adore Aiden, he was annoying me a tad bit in this book. There were a few scenes that I loved, such as the zoo (EEEK that was amazing), the training sessions with Alex, or his constant arguing with Seth. However, he was being a serious jerk. He kept saying he didn't/couldn't love Alex and he didn't mean to kiss her or lead her on; he would act cold towards her, but then he would do or say things that proved he loved her. It was sweet, but also super unfair to Alex!<br />I still ship Aiden with Alex, but I also wouldn't mind if she ended up wit Seth, if that makes sense...<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Something else I wanted to mention was Caleb's death. It was so heartbreaking, as he was a character that I really liked. He was super supportive, kind, protective, funny, and caring, and I'm very sad to see him gone. However, I liked how Seth was so protective of Alex after that happened and stayed with her the whole time. So something sort of good did come out of the terrible at least. <br />Though I must say, I was very shocked and upset with the way Olivia treated Alex after Caleb's death. I liked her character before, but now I don't like her at all. I can't believe she would blame Alex. I mean, it wasn't even her idea to have a movie night. <br /><br />Also, I'm really interested to see who it is that was trying to kill Alex or get her turned into a servant. I have a feeling that it my be Laaden, but I'm not sure. She is kind to Alex and knew her mother, but there's something very suspicious about the whole situation. <br /><br />I'm liking this whole thing with the oracle and all her weird prophecies. They're a bit difficult to understand but I find their role in the plot to be so interesting and I can't wait to learn more about them!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />And can we just take a few moments to appreciate how ultra bad ass Alex was in this book? She seriously kicked butt. That scene at the end with the furies, damn girl! You go! <br />I'm also liking how much she's growing and maturing as a person. While she is still a bit arrogant and disrespectful, as well as flat out stupid at times, she is also very brave and fierce. I loved the part where she showed her scars from being tagged to the Council. She is very tough, and I like that about her.<br /><br />I could honestly ramble on and on about how much I adored this book, but I've got three more books to read in this series! The point is, it was amazing and you need to read this series. Now. <br /><br /><b> February 2019: </b> I still love this series so much. It's just so... good. It's that simple.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3230077444738061315" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17678921476572401486">Oh yes and yet another beautifully crafted book!!   <span id="freeText17678921476572401486" style="display:none">Oh yes and yet another beautifully crafted book!! I just love how much this book made me laugh, oh but don't get me wrong it had me feeling every other emotion possible maybe even some that aren't possible, it even made me cry and boy did I cry at the heart wrenching events that occurred.... Also Alex was so alone in the beginning with the exception of her one true friend Caleb, it's nice to see that her family- what's left of it is starting to care for her truly it is.... <div id="review_878058048" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/878058048" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/878058048?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=audioread">audioread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=alpha-male-love">alpha-male-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer878058048" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15111875010506723143"> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422331269i/13486855.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Pure is book two in the Covenant series. The action is magnified and the tension between Aiden and Alex is like a rubber band ready to snap. And there there is her "other half" Seth. Seth is always lurking around. He is like that presence that will always be there no matter how uncomfortable or happy it makes you. Alex is confused by the comfort she finds being with Seth. And yet, Aiden is all she truly wants.<br/><br/> <b>"Nothing separated us. I tried to breathe, but he had stolen not just my heart, but t</b></span>
  <span id="freeText15111875010506723143" style="display:none"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422331269i/13486855.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Pure is book two in the Covenant series. The action is magnified and the tension between Aiden and Alex is like a rubber band ready to snap. And there there is her "other half" Seth. Seth is always lurking around. He is like that presence that will always be there no matter how uncomfortable or happy it makes you. Alex is confused by the comfort she finds being with Seth. And yet, Aiden is all she truly wants.<br><br> <b>"Nothing separated us. I tried to breathe, but he had stolen not just my heart, but the very air I needed."<b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422331269i/13486856.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Just when Alex thinks that Aiden might be falling in love with her, he pulls away. It is heart breaking to watch her live day to day with out him. Seth tries to fill the vacancy of her heart and yet no one can fill this void! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422331269i/13486857._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Alex is swept away to the covenant in New York. There she faces many trials. She realizes the magnitude of her destiny. Seth continues to train Alex and the training begins to hurt her. While in New York, she attends a ball. When Aiden sees her, he is reminded of what they have both been forced to give up!<br><br><b>"...slowly, almost reluctantly, Aiden looked over his shoulder. The moment our eyes met, I felt like Cinderella."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422331269i/13486858._SY540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So many things happen in this book. One thing is for sure: Alex is in danger, she is madly in love with Aiden, and Seth is not exactly who we thought he was.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422331269i/13486859.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As Aiden makes the ultimate sacrifice for Alex, his true feelings for her are revealed. Luckily for me, the entire series is already out! On to the next book! <br><br><b>“There are always choices.” </b></b></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="15111875010506723143" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
