<div id="review_224307265" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/224307265" />
    <a title="Sherbie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5095949-sherbie"><img alt="Sherbie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1401593782p2/5095949.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/224307265?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sherbie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sherbie" href="/user/show/5095949-sherbie">Sherbie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13543570-pure">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Paranormal Romance lovers/ YA readers/ those who do not want to waste time reading crappy books</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5095949-sherbie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5095949-sherbie?shelf=just-so-awesome">just-so-awesome</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5095949-sherbie?shelf=series-me-loves">series-me-loves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5095949-sherbie?shelf=most-romantic-getaway">most-romantic-getaway</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer224307265" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15812292798999792277"><i>
  <b>She opened her eyes. "Is this real?"<br/>"Very real." I brushed the soaked strands off her cheek, wondering if I was lying or not and if I should care if I was. "Angel, let me kiss you."<br/>-Seth POV #prematureventricularcontractions<br/><br/>“You'll become the center of someone's world one day. <br/>And he'll be the luckiest son of a bitch on this earth.” <br/>-Aiden (i know, i know. and it wont be with you! shoo!)</b>
</i><br/><br/><u>This book for me, was the epitome of YA paranormal/romance.</u><br/>This was even better than the first book of the</span>
  <span id="freeText15812292798999792277" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>She opened her eyes. "Is this real?"<br />"Very real." I brushed the soaked strands off her cheek, wondering if I was lying or not and if I should care if I was. "Angel, let me kiss you."<br />-Seth POV #prematureventricularcontractions<br /><br />“You'll become the center of someone's world one day. <br />And he'll be the luckiest son of a bitch on this earth.” <br />-Aiden (i know, i know. and it wont be with you! shoo!)</b>
</i><br /><br /><u>This book for me, was the epitome of YA paranormal/romance.</u><br />This was even better than the first book of the series.<br />I started on it last night and read 'til my eyes stung.<br />Then read it the whole day today. Yeah, even though I was completely aware that I had this major test coming this thursday.<br />I just had to make time for this book.<br />I fell for this book hard, <b>Jennifer Armentrout did not know how to disappoint.</b><br />When I saw that this book had more pages than Half-Blood did, I sighed with happiness. <br />With a story like this, the more pages the better. <br />Yes I kind of felt the deja vu sensation when reading some parts of the story.<br />But do I give single damn?! <b>NO.</b><br />Why? <u>Because of the immaculate, clever, strongest, hotness incarnate Apollyon.</u><br />Love of my life. <br />Damn girl. Stick with him and try your hardest to get over Aiden.<br />Sighhhhh... Seth. My Seth.... <br />Fated love it is. I enjoyed every part of the story that he was in. <br />This was such a treat for me, especially the scene in the swimming pool. ;)<br />I devoured it like a chocolate cake. &lt;3<br /><br />The pace was perfect, again. The plot, just complete awesomeness.<br />Alex continued being one of the toughest heroines out there.<br />I also had to give credits to Aiden. He was brave and strong enough to do what was right for the both of them. But I still cant bring myself to choose him over Seth. Aiden was a bit boring for me.<br /><br />Heartbreaking at some, thrilling and just so fecking sweet at most.<br /><b>And badass through and through.</b><br />I cried once. xoxo<br /><br />----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br />I AM DYING TO READ THIS!!! Choosing between a fated and forbidden love?! Bring it on! &lt;3</span>
  <a data-text-id="15812292798999792277" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('XdiOW1VzQfqszG87KvexEEGRdOc1BjgqDH3lr7apUPxn/ueJ7i2Ikgvn21rdArvPl86TL/uLtk1XA6Mee+qiZg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CB2HCYAxv2RkLAt2VuG19gSRLMzAVFrXa4To7l/qDW0yO+7bO292DMMHvxehFL8p0s7LBA7Z1LAw+q5fkqn/9w==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText1263602006025430094" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>
